# History of Present Illness

 is a 67 year-old non-hispanic white male. # Social History

 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

 is a 67 year-old non-hispanic white male. Patient has a history of part-time employment (finding), not in labor force (finding), limited social contact (finding), unhealthy alcohol drinking behavior (finding), reports of violence in the environment (finding), full-time employment (finding), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), stress (finding), social isolation (finding), severe anxiety (panic) (finding.

# Social History
Patient is married. Patient is temporarily homeless. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has NO INSURANCE.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications

- Blurred Vision
- urinary frequency
- Fatigue
- Frequent Urination


# History of Present Illness
Robert
 is a 65 year-old non-hispanic white male. Patient has a history of part-time employment (finding), not in labor force (finding), limited social contact (finding), unhealthy alcohol drinking behavior (finding), reports of violence in the environment (finding), full-time employment (finding), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), stress (finding), social isolation (finding), severe anxiety (panic) (finding.

# Social History
Patient is married. Patient is temporarily homeless. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has NO INSURANCE.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet; 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]; simvastatin 10 mg oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The following procedures were conducted:
- renal dialysis (procedure)
The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]

 is a 64 year-old non-hispanic white male. Patient has a history of part-time employment (finding), not in labor force (finding), limited social contact (finding), unhealthy alcohol drinking behavior (finding), reports of violence in the environment (finding), full-time employment (finding), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), stress (finding), social isolation (finding), severe anxiety (panic) (finding.

# Social History
Patient is married. Patient is temporarily homeless. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has NO INSURANCE.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet; 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]; simvastatin 10 mg oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan

The following procedures were conducted:
- assessment of health and social care needs (procedure)
The patient was prescribed the following medications:
- insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]
- hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet
- lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet

- Blurred Vision
- urinary frequency
- Fatigue
- Frequent Urination


# History of Present Illness
Robert
 is a 63 year-old non-hispanic white male. Patient has a history of part-time employment (finding), not in labor force (finding), limited social contact (finding), unhealthy alcohol drinking behavior (finding), reports of violence in the environment (finding), full-time employment (finding), victim of intimate partner abuse (finding), stress (finding), social isolation (finding), severe anxiety (panic) (finding.

# Social History
Patient is married. Patient is temporarily homeless. Patient is an active smoker and is an alcoholic.
 Patient identifies as heterosexual.

Patient comes from a middle socioeconomic background.
 Patient has completed some college courses.
Patient currently has NO INSURANCE.

# Allergies
No Known Allergies.

# Medications
lisinopril 10 mg oral tablet; 1 ml epoetin alfa 4000 unt/ml injection [epogen]; simvastatin 10 mg oral tablet; hydrochlorothiazide 25 mg oral tablet; insulin human, isophane 70 unt/ml / regular insulin, human 30 unt/ml injectable suspension [humulin]

# Assessment and Plan


## Plan
